<username>Jules Nuggy</username><Date>1560267047823< /Date><rating>4< /rating>< Review>
Visited 10 June 2019. Lovely food here - I had the pho tai nam and it's pretty amazing. The broth is on point - flavoursome, good colour, and clean. They were very generous with the meat portions and at $12 for a large is great value. Also had the spring rolls (which are actually what I would call summer rolls) and they were delicious and, again, a good portion for the price of $8. My boyfriend had the Vietnamese salad with calamari and he kept finding more and more calamari as he worked through it!

Our server was very friendly and she was very helpful with advising us on the dishes and how much to order.

Minus one star for the insane temperatures inside the restaurant due to lack of Aircon. It was so hot I felt like I was actually in Vietnam, sweating like mad!</Review>

<review>If you're not Salvadorian, you don't understand the cultural significance and nostalgia it brings to Salvis. It's a popular bakery in El Salvador, so I value this place and the workers because my family from El Salvador find joy in the bread from here. I have family in Novato who drive down just to pick up this bread and family in Los Angeles who asks to bring this bread when we visit. The pasteles de leche are my favorite and I always make sure to also get some tamales de pollo with bolios for breakfast! You can't go wrong with what you get, they have sweet bread for multiple all different lovers of the best carbs!

The owner is my favorite person and he's always there when I go, I love being able to have a conversation with him about life! When I first moved here 10 years ago, my parents discovered this place for the first time and my dad told him to look after me when they go back to LA. Lol that's the Salvi way, we are connected through the love for the country that everyone is like family, even if you just met for the first time! Going here makes me feel more at home! And did I mention the pasteles de leche and tamales de pollo?! Delicious!

Great bread, great humans!< /review>< pics>
None<//pics>

<user>110646334169299791256</user><review>Thankfully Deciem's erratic founder no longer seems to be involved, so I don't think this store is going anywhere soon (all stores were spontaneously shut down a while ago on the former CEO's command). If you're looking for a quick and easy way to improve your skincare routine, this is it. I love how straightforward their products are, with transparent labeling. Other brands try to dazzle you with catchy phrases like "patented anti-aging technologies", without detailing percentages of active ingredients.

Though small, this shop offers all their product lines; however, they have a very limited supply, so maybe call in advance if you wanted anything in particular. The clerks are very friendly and helpful, but do your research before coming to the store. The first time I came, I asked if niacinimide would help even my skin tone; I was told it's only meant to reduce pores and control oiliness, so I shouldn't use it because my skin isn't oily...

I've been using their stuff for about half a year now, and I'm pretty pleased with the results. Their retinoid helped clear up some closed comedones, and I use their face oils nightly. The seabuckthorn oil will stain everything you love orange, but it hydrates nicely.<//review></record>

<Rate>5<//Rate><Text>I buy The Ordinary products from their online store and am so excited that the parent company Deciem recently opened a location here in SF. Finding the right products for my sensitive skin is difficult due to many that contain irritants like fragrances and essential oils, which have no benefits in skincare at all. Thankfully, TO provides effective skincare ingredients in product form at an affordable price. My skin has seen noticable effects in improvement after a month or two (your mileage may vary so patch test first to check if compatible with your skin).

They have an excellent one year return policy--they know that products take time to show effects on skin.

Some popular products, like the niacinamide, do run out at times, so make sure to call the store beforehand to check if a product you want is in stock. There are testers for every product in the store, even for ones that are out of stock.

The employees are knowledgeable and helpful! Everything might seem overwhelming at first if you're new to the brand,  so the employees are there to help address any questions and concerns.

There was a sign at checkout saying that they don't accept cash at the moment. Just letting you know.</Text><pics>None</pics>< Resp>
